				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Lachrimae, or Seven Tears (Dowland, John)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div><table style="padding:0.5em; margin-left:auto; margin-right:auto; background-color:rgb(245,245,245); width:70%; border:1px solid #a3bfb1"><tr><td width="42px" valign="top"><a href="/wiki/File:Ambox_notice.png" class="image"><img alt="Ambox notice.png" src="/images/c/c8/Ambox_notice.png" width="40" height="40" /></a></td><td align="center">
This page is <b>only</b> for <b>complete</b> editions and <b>multiple selections</b> from the collection here. For arrangements, new editions, and the like see (or create) separate pages for individual works linked in the <b>General Information</b> section below.</td></tr></table></div>

<td>1605

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Lachrimae, or Seven Tears
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head"><i>Title-page transcription</i> <span class="expandline">Lachrimae, or Seaven Teares figvred in Seaven Passionate Pauans, with diuers other Pauans, Galiards, and Almands, set forth for the Lute, Viols, or Violons, in fiue parts: By Iohn Dowland Bachelor of Musicke, and Lutenist to the most Royall and Magnificent, Christian the fourth, King of Denmarke, Norway, Vandales, and Gothes, Duke of Sleswicke, Holsten, Stormaria, and Ditmarsh: Earle of Oldenburge and Delmenhorst.</span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Dowland,_John" title="Category:Dowland, John">Dowland, John</a>
</td></tr>
<tr class="udelonly" data-display="table-row">
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>None <small>[<span class="icatassign">force assignment</span>]</small>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>21 pieces
<dl><dd>1. <a href="/wiki/Lachrimae_antiquae_(Dowland,_John)" title="Lachrimae antiquae (Dowland, John)">Lachrimae antiquae</a>
</dd><dd>2. <a href="/wiki/Lachrimae_antiquae_novae_(Dowland,_John)" title="Lachrimae antiquae novae (Dowland, John)">Lachrimae antiquae novae</a>
</dd><dd>3. <a href="/wiki/Lachrimae_gementes_(Dowland,_John)" title="Lachrimae gementes (Dowland, John)">Lachrimae gementes</a>
</dd><dd>4. <a href="/wiki/Lachrimae_tristes_(Dowland,_John)" title="Lachrimae tristes (Dowland, John)">Lachrimae tristes</a>
</dd><dd>5. <a href="/wiki/Lachrimae_coactae_(Dowland,_John)" title="Lachrimae coactae (Dowland, John)">Lachrimae coactae</a>
</dd><dd>6. <a href="/wiki/Lachrimae_amantis_(Dowland,_John)" title="Lachrimae amantis (Dowland, John)">Lachrimae amantis</a>
</dd><dd>7. <a href="/wiki/Lachrimae_verae_(Dowland,_John)" title="Lachrimae verae (Dowland, John)">Lachrimae verae</a>
</dd><dd>8. <a href="/wiki/Semper_Dowland_semper_dolens_(Dowland,_John)" title="Semper Dowland semper dolens (Dowland, John)">Semper Dowland semper dolens</a>
</dd><dd>9. <a href="/wiki/Sir_Henry_Umpton%27s_Funeral_(Dowland,_John)" title="Sir Henry Umpton's Funeral (Dowland, John)">Sir Henry Umpton's Funeral</a>
</dd><dd>10. <a href="/wiki/Mr._John_Langton%27s_Pavan_(Dowland,_John)" title="Mr. John Langton's Pavan (Dowland, John)">Mr. John Langton's Pavan</a>
</dd><dd>11. <a href="/wiki/The_King_of_Denmark%27s_Galliard_(Dowland,_John)" title="The King of Denmark's Galliard (Dowland, John)">The King of Denmark's Galliard</a>

</dd><dd>17. <a href="/wiki/Mr._Thomas_Collier_his_Galliard_(Dowland,_John)" title="Mr. Thomas Collier his Galliard (Dowland, John)">Mr. Thomas Collier his Galliard</a> (with 2 trebles)
</dd><dd>18. <a href="/wiki/Captain_Digorie_Piper_his_Galliard_(Dowland,_John)" title="Captain Digorie Piper his Galliard (Dowland, John)">Captain Digorie Piper his Galliard</a>
